2009-11-24 Finally the corrected tagAligns
==========================================
Several problems were fixed by hand editing DAF/DDFs
1) Mike Wilson submitted DDFs with multiple lines per dataset!
2) The DAF matchFirst had to change from 32 to 30.
3) Several types such as Jun instead of c-Jun
4) He include PolyA RNA which is a no no.
To solve this I create an rna subdir for 634, then move the data files and create a daf/ddf.
Then
tar -cpzf YDH_RnaSeq_tagAlign_update.tgz *  
submitted as 788
Notice that 276 is marked as released but it is only displayed
update projects set status = 'displayed' where id = 276;

select distinct t1.val cell,t2.val treatment,t3.val antibody,t4.val input,t5.val inputType from mdb_tdreszer t1,mdb_tdreszer t2,mdb_tdreszer t3,mdb_tdreszer t4,mdb_tdreszer t5 where t1.obj like "wgEncodeYaleChIP%"
 and t1.obj = t2.obj and t2.obj = t3.obj and t3.obj = t4.obj and t4.obj = t5.obj
 and t1.var = "cell" and t2.var = "treatment" and t3.var = "antibody" and t4.var = "input" and t5.var = "inputType"
 order by t5.val,t4.val,t1.val,t2.val,t3.val;

mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder inputType=%MNase" -var=control -val=MNase
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder inputType=%IgG-mus" -var=control -val=IgG-mus
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder inputType=%IgG-rab" -var=control -val=IgG-rab
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder inputType=%Naked_DNA" -var=control -val=Naked_DNA
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder inputType=%Large_Fragment" -var=control -val=Large_Fragment
mdbPrint hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder" -ra > mdbYaleTfbs.ra
mdbUpdate hg18 -table=mdb mdbYaleTfbs.ra
cvs ci mdbYaleTfbs.ra

## Fix at last K562b/None/SETDB1/MNase
# MNase in this case is a treatment (sort of)!
# Register a treatment MNaseD (MNase is a control term!)
mdbPrint hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder cell=K562b treatment=None antibody=SETDB1 inputType=%MNase" > tmpMNase.ra
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder cell=K562b treatment=None antibody=SETDB1 inputType=%MNase" -var=treatment -val=MNaseD -test
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder cell=K562b treatment=MNaseD antibody=SETDB1 inputType=%MNase" -var=inputType -val=K562b/None/Input/UCDavis -test
mdbUpdate hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder cell=K562b treatment=MNaseD antibody=SETDB1" -var=control -val=UCDavis -test
mdbPrint hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder cell=K562b treatment=MNaseD antibody=SETDB1" > tmpMNase2.ra
diff tmpMNase.ra tmpMNase2.ra 
mdbPrint hg18 -vars="grant=Snyder" > mdbYaleTfbs.ra 
Using table named 'hg18.mdb_tdreszer'.
objects:1073  vars:22410
mdbUpdate hg18 -table=mdb mdbYaleTfbs.ra 
Using table named 'hg18.mdb_tdreszer'.
Read 1073 metadata objects from hg18
Affected 0 row(s) in hg18.mdb_tdreszer
cvs ci -m "Straightened out Yale K562/None/SETDB1/MNase at last" mdbYaleTfbs.ra
